    "new_string": "'use client'\n\nimport { useState, useEffect, useCallback, useMemo, useRef } from 'react';\nimport type { NextPage } from 'next';\n\n// --- Interfaces ---\n\n\n// --- Default Data (will be loaded if no data exists) ---\nconst createDefaultDeck = (): Deck => ({\n    id: 'default_deck_1',\n    name: 'Sample React/Web Dev Deck',\n    cards: [\n        { id: 1, front: \"What is React?\", back: \"A JavaScript library for building user interfaces.\", tags: [\"react\", \"frontend\", \"javascript\"] },\n        { id: 2, front: \"What is useState?\", back: \"A React Hook that lets you add state to functional components.\", tags: [\"react\", \"hooks\"] },\n        { id: 3, front: \"What is Tailwind CSS?\", back: \"A utility-first CSS framework.\", tags: [\"css\", \"frontend\", \"styling\"] },\n        { id: 4, front: \"What is TypeScript?\", back: \"A typed superset of JavaScript.\", tags: [\"javascript\", \"typing\"] },\n        { id: 5, front: \"Purpose of useEffect?\", back: \"To perform side effects in functional components.\", tags: [\"react\", \"hooks\", \"side-effects\"] },\n        { id: 6, front: \"What is JSX?\", back: \"A syntax extension for JavaScript, used with React.\", tags: [\"react\", \"javascript\"] },\n        { id: 7, front: \"CSS Box Model (Order)\", back: \"Content, Padding, Border, Margin\", tags: [\"css\", \"frontend\", \"styling\"] },\n        { id: 8, front: \"What is 'git clone'?\", back: \"Command to create a local copy of a remote repository.\", tags: [\"git\", \"version-control\"] },\n        { id: 9, front: \"What is 'git push'?\", back: \"Command to upload local repository content to a remote repository.\", tags: [\"git\", \"version-control\"] },\n        // Your Machine Learning Deck - incorporate it here or upload it\n        // { id: 10, front: \"What is Supervised Learning?\", back: \"Predict output Y from input X (Regression/Classification).\", tags: [\"Supervised Learning\", \"Core Concept\"] },\n        // ... add more ML cards or keep separate for upload demo\n    ],\n    tagScores: { /* 'strong-tag': { correct: 10, incorrect: 0 } */ } // Example initial score\n});\n\n// --- LocalStorage Keys ---\nconst LS_ALL_DECKS_KEY = 'flashcard_allDecks';\nconst LS_SELECTED_DECK_ID_KEY = 'flashcard_selectedDeckId';\n\n// --- Helper: Generate Unique ID ---\nconst generateDeckId = () => `deck_${Date.now()}_${Math.random().toString(36).substring(2, 7)}`;\n\n// --- The App Component ---\nconst FlashcardApp: NextPage = () => {\n    // --- State ---\n    const [allDecks, setAllDecks] = useState<AllDecks>({});\n    const [selectedDeckId, setSelectedDeckId] = useState<string | null>(null);\n    const [shuffledIndices, setShuffledIndices] = useState<number[]>([]);\n    const [currentShuffledIndex, setCurrentShuffledIndex] = useState<number>(0);\n    const [isFlipped, setIsFlipped] = useState<boolean>(false);\n    const [view, setView] = useState<View>('viewer');\n    const [editingDeckId, setEditingDeckId] = useState<string | null>(null); // Track which deck name is being edited\n    const [tempDeckName, setTempDeckName] = useState<string>('');\n    const fileInputRef = useRef<HTMLInputElement>(null); // Ref for file input\n\n    // --- Persistence ---\n    useEffect(() => {\n        // Load data on initial mount\n        const savedDecks = localStorage.getItem(LS_ALL_DECKS_KEY);\n        const savedSelectedId = localStorage.getItem(LS_SELECTED_DECK_ID_KEY);\n        let loadedDecks: AllDecks = {};\n        let loadedSelectedId: string | null = null;\n\n        if (savedDecks) {\n            try {\n                loadedDecks = JSON.parse(savedDecks);\n            } catch (e) {\n                console.error(\"Failed to parse saved decks:\", e);\n            }\n        }\n\n        // If no decks loaded, create the default one\n        if (Object.keys(loadedDecks).length === 0) {\n            const defaultDeck = createDefaultDeck();\n            loadedDecks = { [defaultDeck.id]: defaultDeck };\n            loadedSelectedId = defaultDeck.id; // Select the default deck initially\n        } else if (savedSelectedId && loadedDecks[savedSelectedId]) {\n            loadedSelectedId = savedSelectedId;\n        } else {\n            // If saved ID is invalid or missing, select the first available deck\n            loadedSelectedId = Object.keys(loadedDecks)[0] || null;\n        }\n\n        setAllDecks(loadedDecks);\n        setSelectedDeckId(loadedSelectedId);\n    }, []);\n\n    useEffect(() => {\n        // Save decks whenever they change\n        if (Object.keys(allDecks).length > 0) {\n            localStorage.setItem(LS_ALL_DECKS_KEY, JSON.stringify(allDecks));\n        } else {\n            // Clear if empty to avoid storing \"{}\"\n            localStorage.removeItem(LS_ALL_DECKS_KEY);\n        }\n    }, [allDecks]);\n\n    useEffect(() => {\n        // Save selected deck ID whenever it changes\n        if (selectedDeckId) {\n            localStorage.setItem(LS_SELECTED_DECK_ID_KEY, selectedDeckId);\n        } else {\n            localStorage.removeItem(LS_SELECTED_DECK_ID_KEY);\n        }\n    }, [selectedDeckId]);\n\n    // --- Derived State (Current Deck Data) ---\n    const currentDeck = useMemo(() => {\n        if (!selectedDeckId || !allDecks[selectedDeckId]) return null;\n        return allDecks[selectedDeckId];\n    }, [allDecks, selectedDeckId]);\n\n    const cards = useMemo(() => currentDeck?.cards ?? [], [currentDeck]);\n    const tagScores = useMemo(() => currentDeck?.tagScores ?? {}, [currentDeck]);\n    const deckName = useMemo(() => currentDeck?.name ?? 'No Deck Selected', [currentDeck]);\n\n    // --- Shuffling Logic (Adapted) ---\n    const getTagPerformance = useCallback((tag: string): number => {\n        const score = tagScores[tag] || { correct: 0, incorrect: 0 };\n        const total = score.correct + score.incorrect;\n        if (total === 0) return 0.5; // Neutral score for unseen tags\n        return score.correct / total;\n    }, [tagScores]); // Depends on the tagScores of the *current* deck\n\n    const getCardWeakness = useCallback((card: Card): number => {\n        if (!card.tags || card.tags.length === 0) return 0.5; // Neutral for untagged cards\n        const performances = card.tags.map(getTagPerformance);\n        return Math.min(...performances); // Weakness is determined by the weakest tag\n    }, [getTagPerformance]);\n\n    const shuffleDeck = useCallback(() => {\n        if (!cards || cards.length === 0) {\n            setShuffledIndices([]);\n            setCurrentShuffledIndex(0);\n            return;\n        }\n        const indices = cards.map((_, index) => index);\n        indices.sort((indexA, indexB) => {\n            const cardA = cards[indexA];\n            const cardB = cards[indexB];\n            const weaknessA = getCardWeakness(cardA);\n            const weaknessB = getCardWeakness(cardB);\n            // Primary sort: weakness ascending (weakest first)\n            // Secondary sort: random shuffle for cards with equal weakness\n            if (weaknessA !== weaknessB) {\n                return weaknessA - weaknessB;\n            } else {\n                return Math.random() - 0.5;\n            }\n        });\n        setShuffledIndices(indices);\n        setCurrentShuffledIndex(0);\n        setIsFlipped(false);\n        console.log(\"Shuffled. Weakest first based on tags:\", indices.map(i => cards[i]?.front ?? 'N/A'));\n    }, [cards, getCardWeakness]); // Depends on the cards of the *current* deck\n\n    useEffect(() => {\n        // Re-shuffle when the selected deck changes or cards within it change\n        // console.log(\"Deck changed or cards updated, shuffling...\");\n        shuffleDeck();\n    }, [selectedDeckId, cards, shuffleDeck]); // Ensure cards is a dependency\n\n    // --- Card Navigation & Scoring (Adapted) ---\n    const currentCardIndex = shuffledIndices[currentShuffledIndex];\n    const currentCard = cards[currentCardIndex];\n\n    const handleAnswer = (isCorrect: boolean) => {\n        if (!currentCard || !selectedDeckId) return;\n\n        setAllDecks(prevAllDecks => {\n            const deckToUpdate = prevAllDecks[selectedDeckId];\n            if (!deckToUpdate) return prevAllDecks; // Should not happen if selectedDeckId is valid\n\n            const newScores = { ...(deckToUpdate.tagScores || {}) };\n            (currentCard.tags ?? []).forEach(tag => {\n                const score = newScores[tag] || { correct: 0, incorrect: 0 };\n                if (isCorrect) {\n                    score.correct += 1;\n                } else {\n                    score.incorrect += 1;\n                }\n                newScores[tag] = { ...score }; // Ensure new object for state update\n            });\n\n            const updatedDeck = { ...deckToUpdate, tagScores: newScores };\n            return { ...prevAllDecks, [selectedDeckId]: updatedDeck };\n        });\n\n        goToNextCard();\n    };\n\n    const goToNextCard = () => {\n        if (shuffledIndices.length === 0) return;\n        setIsFlipped(false);\n        // Trigger re-shuffle if it's the last card and user wraps around (optional)\n        // if (currentShuffledIndex === shuffledIndices.length - 1) {\n        //     shuffleDeck();\n        // } else {\n        setCurrentShuffledIndex(prev => (prev + 1) % shuffledIndices.length);\n        // }\n    };\n\n    const goToPrevCard = () => {\n        if (shuffledIndices.length === 0) return;\n        setIsFlipped(false);\n        setCurrentShuffledIndex(prev => (prev - 1 + shuffledIndices.length) % shuffledIndices.length);\n    };\n\n    // --- Deck Management Logic ---\n    const handleFileUpload = (event: React.ChangeEvent<HTMLInputElement>) => {\n        const file = event.target.files?.[0];\n        if (!file) return;\n\n        const reader = new FileReader();\n        reader.onload = (e) => {\n            try {\n                const content = e.target?.result;\n                if (typeof content !== 'string') throw new Error(\"Failed to read file content.\");\n\n                const parsedCards: Card[] = JSON.parse(content);\n\n                // Basic validation\n                if (!Array.isArray(parsedCards) || parsedCards.some(c => !c.front || !c.back)) {\n                    throw new Error(\"Invalid JSON format. Expected an array of objects with 'front' and 'back' properties.\");\n                }\n\n                // Ensure tags is an array if present\n                const validatedCards = parsedCards.map((card, index) => ({\n                    ...card,\n                    id: card.id ?? `card_${index}`, // Assign index-based ID if missing\n                    tags: Array.isArray(card.tags) ? card.tags : [], // Default to empty array if tags missing/invalid\n                }));\n\n\n                const newDeckId = generateDeckId();\n                const newDeckName = file.name.replace(/\\.[^/.]+$/, \"\") || `Uploaded Deck ${Object.keys(allDecks).length + 1}`; // Use filename as name\n                const newDeck: Deck = {\n                    id: newDeckId,\n                    name: newDeckName,\n                    cards: validatedCards,\n                    tagScores: {}, // Initialize empty scores\n                };\n\n                setAllDecks(prev => ({ ...prev, [newDeckId]: newDeck }));\n                setSelectedDeckId(newDeckId); // Select the newly uploaded deck\n                setView('viewer'); // Switch back to viewer\n                alert(`Deck \"${newDeckName}\" uploaded successfully with ${validatedCards.length} cards!`);\n\n            } catch (error) {\n                console.error(\"Error processing JSON file:\", error);\n                alert(`Error uploading file: ${error instanceof Error ? error.message : \"Unknown error\"}`);\n            } finally {\n                // Reset file input value to allow uploading the same file again\n                if (fileInputRef.current) {\n                    fileInputRef.current.value = '';\n                }\n            }\n        };\n        reader.onerror = () => {\n            alert(\"Error reading file.\");\n            if (fileInputRef.current) {\n                fileInputRef.current.value = '';\n            }\n        };\n        reader.readAsText(file);\n    };\n\n    const handleSelectDeck = (deckId: string) => {\n        if (allDecks[deckId]) {\n            setSelectedDeckId(deckId);\n            setView('viewer'); // Go to viewer when selecting a deck\n            // Shuffle will be triggered by useEffect dependency change\n        }\n    };\n\n    const handleDeleteDeck = (deckId: string) => {\n        if (!allDecks[deckId]) return;\n        const deckToDeleteName = allDecks[deckId].name;\n        if (window.confirm(`Are you sure you want to delete the deck \"${deckToDeleteName}\"? This cannot be undone.`)) {\n            setAllDecks(prev => {\n                const newState = { ...prev };\n                delete newState[deckId];\n                return newState;\n            });\n            // If the deleted deck was selected, select another one or null\n            if (selectedDeckId === deckId) {\n                const remainingIds = Object.keys(allDecks).filter(id => id !== deckId);\n                setSelectedDeckId(remainingIds[0] || null);\n                // If no decks left, viewer will show \"No Deck Selected\"\n            }\n        }\n    };\n\n    const handleDeckNameEdit = (deckId: string) => {\n        setTempDeckName(allDecks[deckId]?.name ?? '');\n        setEditingDeckId(deckId);\n    };\n\n    const handleDeckNameSave = () => {\n        if (!editingDeckId || !tempDeckName.trim()) return;\n        setAllDecks(prev => {\n            const deckToUpdate = prev[editingDeckId];\n            if (!deckToUpdate) return prev;\n            return { ...prev, [editingDeckId]: { ...deckToUpdate, name: tempDeckName.trim() } };\n        });\n        setEditingDeckId(null);\n        setTempDeckName('');\n    };\n\n    const handleDeckNameCancel = () => {\n        setEditingDeckId(null);\n        setTempDeckName('');\n    };\n\n    // --- Stats (Adapted) ---\n    const sortedTags = useMemo(() => {\n        return Object.entries(tagScores) // Uses tagScores derived from currentDeck\n            .map(([tag, score]) => ({\n                tag,\n                ...score,\n                performance: (score.correct + score.incorrect) === 0 ? 0.5 : score.correct / (score.correct + score.incorrect),\n                total: score.correct + score.incorrect\n            }))\n            .sort((a, b) => a.performance - b.performance); // Weakest first\n    }, [tagScores]); // Depends only on current deck's scores\n\n    const resetTagScore = (tag: string) => {\n        if (!selectedDeckId) return;\n        setAllDecks(prevAllDecks => {\n            const deckToUpdate = prevAllDecks[selectedDeckId];\n            if (!deckToUpdate || !deckToUpdate.tagScores || !deckToUpdate.tagScores[tag]) return prevAllDecks;\n\n            const newScores = { ...deckToUpdate.tagScores };\n            delete newScores[tag]; // Remove the specific tag score\n\n            const updatedDeck = { ...deckToUpdate, tagScores: newScores };\n            return { ...prevAllDecks, [selectedDeckId]: updatedDeck };\n        });\n    };\n\n    // --- Settings (Adapted) ---\n    const resetCurrentDeckScores = () => {\n        if (!selectedDeckId || !currentDeck) return;\n        if (window.confirm(`Are you sure you want to reset all tag scores for the deck \"${deckName}\"?`)) {\n            setAllDecks(prevAllDecks => {\n                const deckToUpdate = prevAllDecks[selectedDeckId];\n                if (!deckToUpdate) return prevAllDecks; // Should not happen\n\n                const updatedDeck = { ...deckToUpdate, tagScores: {} }; // Reset scores to empty object\n                return { ...prevAllDecks, [selectedDeckId]: updatedDeck };\n            });\n        }\n    };\n\n    const clearAllData = () => {\n        if (window.confirm(\"DELETE ALL DATA?\\n\\nAre you sure you want to clear all decks and scores? This cannot be undone.\")) {\n            setAllDecks({});\n            setSelectedDeckId(null);\n            localStorage.removeItem(LS_ALL_DECKS_KEY);\n            localStorage.removeItem(LS_SELECTED_DECK_ID_KEY);\n            // Optionally load default deck again after clearing\n            // const defaultDeck = createDefaultDeck();\n            // setAllDecks({ [defaultDeck.id]: defaultDeck });\n            // setSelectedDeckId(defaultDeck.id);\n            alert(\"All data cleared.\");\n            setView('manage_decks'); // Go to manage decks view after clearing\n        }\n    };\n\n    // --- Render ---\n    return (\n        <div className=\"min-h-screen bg-gray-100 text-gray-800 p-4 sm:p-6 lg:p-8 font-sans\">\n            <div className=\"max-w-3xl mx-auto bg-white rounded-lg shadow-lg p-6\">\n                {/* Header & Deck Name Display (Viewer only shows current deck name) */}\n                <div className=\"mb-6 pb-4 border-b border-gray-200 flex flex-col sm:flex-row justify-between items-center gap-4\">\n                    <h1 className=\"text-xl sm:text-2xl font-semibold text-gray-700 truncate text-center sm:text-left\">\n                        {view === 'viewer' || view === 'stats' ? `Studying: ${deckName}` : 'Flashcard App'}\n                        {currentDeck && <span className='text-sm font-normal text-gray-500 ml-2'>({cards.length} cards)</span>}\n                        {!currentDeck && view === 'viewer' && <span className='text-lg font-normal text-red-500'> (No deck selected)</span>}\n                    </h1>\n                    <nav className=\"flex space-x-2 sm:space-x-3 flex-wrap justify-center\">\n                        <button\n                            onClick={() => setView('viewer')}\n                            className={`px-3 py-1 rounded text-sm sm:text-base ${view === 'viewer' ? 'bg-blue-500 text-white' : 'text-blue-600 hover:bg-blue-100'}`}\n                        >\n                            Viewer\n                        </button>\n                        <button\n                            onClick={() => setView('stats')}\n                            className={`px-3 py-1 rounded text-sm sm:text-base ${view === 'stats' ? 'bg-blue-500 text-white' : 'text-blue-600 hover:bg-blue-100'}`}\n                        >\n                            Stats\n                        </button>\n                        <button\n                            onClick={() => setView('manage_decks')}\n                            className={`px-3 py-1 rounded text-sm sm:text-base ${view === 'manage_decks' ? 'bg-blue-500 text-white' : 'text-blue-600 hover:bg-blue-100'}`}\n                        >\n                            Manage Decks\n                        </button>\n                        <button\n                            onClick={() => setView('settings')}\n                            className={`px-3 py-1 rounded text-sm sm:text-base ${view === 'settings' ? 'bg-blue-500 text-white' : 'text-blue-600 hover:bg-blue-100'}`}\n                        >\n                            Settings\n                        </button>\n                    </nav>\n                </div>\n\n                {/* --- Content Area --- */}\n\n                {/* Viewer View */}\n                {view === 'viewer' && (\n                    <div>\n                        {!currentDeck && (\n                            <div className=\"text-center py-10\">\n                                <p className=\"text-xl text-gray-500 mb-4\">No deck selected.</p>\n                                <button\n                                    onClick={() => setView('manage_decks')}\n                                    className=\"px-4 py-2 bg-blue-500 text-white rounded hover:bg-blue-600\"\n                                >\n                                    Go to Manage Decks\n                                </button>\n                            </div>\n                        )}\n                        {currentDeck && currentCard && (\n                            <div className=\"flex flex-col items-center\">\n                                {/* Card Flip Container */}\n                                <div\n                                    className=\"perspective w-full max-w-md h-64 mb-4 cursor-pointer group\"\n                                    onClick={() => setIsFlipped(!isFlipped)}\n                                    role=\"button\" // Accessibility\n                                    tabIndex={0} // Accessibility\n                                    onKeyDown={(e) => (e.key === ' ' || e.key === 'Enter') && setIsFlipped(!isFlipped)} // Accessibility\n                                >\n                                    <div\n                                        className={`relative w-full h-full rounded-lg shadow-md transition-transform duration-700 transform-style-3d ${isFlipped ? 'rotate-y-180' : ''}`}\n                                    >\n                                        {/* Front */}\n                                        <div className=\"absolute w-full h-full backface-hidden bg-blue-100 border border-blue-200 rounded-lg flex items-center justify-center p-6 text-center overflow-auto\">\n                                            <p className=\"text-lg sm:text-xl text-blue-800\">{currentCard.front}</p>\n                                        </div>\n                                        {/* Back */}\n                                        <div className=\"absolute w-full h-full backface-hidden rotate-y-180 bg-green-100 border border-green-200 rounded-lg flex items-center justify-center p-6 text-center overflow-auto\">\n                                            <p className=\"text-lg sm:text-xl text-green-800\">{currentCard.back}</p>\n                                        </div>\n                                    </div>\n                                </div>\n\n                                <button\n                                    onClick={() => setIsFlipped(!isFlipped)}\n                                    className=\"mb-4 px-4 py-2 bg-gray-200 text-gray-700 rounded hover:bg-gray-300 text-sm\"\n                                >\n                                    Flip Card\n                                </button>\n\n                                {/* Answer Buttons */}\n                                <div className=\"flex space-x-4 mb-4\">\n                                    <button\n                                        onClick={() => handleAnswer(false)}\n                                        className=\"px-5 py-2 bg-red-500 text-white rounded hover:bg-red-600 transition-colors font-medium\"\n                                    >\n                                        Incorrect\n                                    </button>\n                                    <button\n                                        onClick={() => handleAnswer(true)}\n                                        className=\"px-5 py-2 bg-green-500 text-white rounded hover:bg-green-600 transition-colors font-medium\"\n                                    >\n                                        Correct\n                                    </button>\n                                </div>\n\n                                {/* Navigation & Info */}\n                                <div className=\"flex items-center space-x-4 mb-4\">\n                                    <button\n                                        onClick={goToPrevCard}\n                                        disabled={shuffledIndices.length <= 1}\n                                        className=\"px-3 py-1 bg-gray-500 text-white rounded hover:bg-gray-600 disabled:opacity-50 disabled:cursor-not-allowed text-sm\"\n                                    >\n                                        Prev\n                                    </button>\n                                    <span className=\"text-gray-600 text-sm\">\n                                        Card {currentShuffledIndex + 1} of {shuffledIndices.length}\n                                    </span>\n                                    <button\n                                        onClick={goToNextCard}\n                                        disabled={shuffledIndices.length <= 1}\n                                        className=\"px-3 py-1 bg-gray-500 text-white rounded hover:bg-gray-600 disabled:opacity-50 disabled:cursor-not-allowed text-sm\"\n                                    >\n                                        Next\n                                    </button>\n                                </div>\n\n                                <div className=\"text-xs text-gray-500 mb-4 max-w-md text-center break-words\">\n                                    Tags: {(currentCard.tags ?? []).join(', ') || 'None'}\n                                </div>\n\n                                <button\n                                    onClick={shuffleDeck}\n                                    className=\"px-4 py-2 bg-purple-500 text-white rounded hover:bg-purple-600 text-sm\"\n                                >\n                                    Shuffle Deck (Weakest First)\n                                </button>\n                            </div>\n                        )}\n                        {currentDeck && !currentCard && cards.length === 0 && (\n                            <p className=\"text-center text-gray-500 py-10\">This deck has no cards.</p>\n                        )}\n                    </div>\n                )}\n\n                {/* Stats View */}\n                {view === 'stats' && (\n                    <div>\n                        <h2 className=\"text-xl font-semibold mb-4 text-gray-700\">Tag Performance for \"{deckName}\"</h2>\n                        {!currentDeck && <p className=\"text-gray-500\">Please select a deck to view stats.</p>}\n                        {currentDeck && sortedTags.length > 0 ? (\n                            <ul className=\"space-y-2\">\n                                {sortedTags.map(({ tag, correct, incorrect, performance, total }) => (\n                                    <li key={tag} className=\"flex justify-between items-center p-3 bg-gray-50 rounded border border-gray-200\">\n                                        <div>\n                                            <span className=\"font-medium text-gray-800 mr-2\">{tag}</span>\n                                            <span className={`text-sm px-2 py-0.5 rounded ${performance < 0.4 ? 'bg-red-100 text-red-700' : performance > 0.7 ? 'bg-green-100 text-green-700' : 'bg-yellow-100 text-yellow-700'}`}>\n                                                {Math.round(performance * 100)}%\n                                            </span>\n                                            <span className=\"text-xs text-gray-500 ml-2\">({correct}/{total})</span>\n                                        </div>\n                                        <button\n                                            onClick={() => resetTagScore(tag)}\n                                            className=\"text-xs text-red-500 hover:text-red-700 ml-4\"\n                                            title={`Reset score for tag: ${tag}`}\n                                        >\n                                            Reset\n                                        </button>\n                                    </li>\n                                ))}\n                            </ul>\n                        ) : currentDeck && (\n                            <p className=\"text-gray-500\">No tag scores recorded yet for this deck. Review some cards!</p>\n                        )}\n                    </div>\n                )}\n\n                {/* Manage Decks View */}\n                {view === 'manage_decks' && (\n                    <div>\n                        <h2 className=\"text-xl font-semibold mb-4 text-gray-700\">Manage Decks</h2>\n\n                        {/* Upload Section */}\n                        <div className=\"mb-6 p-4 border border-dashed border-gray-300 rounded bg-gray-50 text-center\">\n                            <h3 className=\"text-lg font-medium mb-2 text-gray-600\">Upload New Deck</h3>\n                            <p className=\"text-sm text-gray-500 mb-3\">Select a JSON file containing an array of flashcards (objects with 'front' and 'back', optionally 'tags').</p>\n                            <input\n                                type=\"file\"\n                                accept=\".json,application/json\"\n                                onChange={handleFileUpload}\n                                ref={fileInputRef}\n                                className=\"hidden\" // Hide default input, style the button instead\n                                id=\"file-upload-input\"\n                            />\n                            <button\n                                onClick={() => fileInputRef.current?.click()}\n                                className=\"px-4 py-2 bg-indigo-500 text-white rounded hover:bg-indigo-600 text-sm\"\n                            >\n                                Choose JSON File...\n                            </button>\n                        </div>\n\n                        {/* Deck List Section */}\n                        <h3 className=\"text-lg font-medium mb-3 text-gray-600\">Available Decks</h3>\n                        {Object.keys(allDecks).length > 0 ? (\n                            <ul className=\"space-y-3\">\n                                {Object.values(allDecks).map((deck) => (\n                                    <li key={deck.id} className=\"flex flex-col sm:flex-row justify-between items-start sm:items-center p-3 bg-white rounded border border-gray-200 shadow-sm gap-2\">\n                                        {editingDeckId === deck.id ? (\n                                            // Edit Mode\n                                            <div className=\"flex items-center space-x-2 flex-grow\">\n                                                <input\n                                                    type=\"text\"\n                                                    value={tempDeckName}\n                                                    onChange={(e) => setTempDeckName(e.target.value)}\n                                                    className=\"border border-gray-300 rounded px-2 py-1 text-sm font-medium flex-grow\"\n                                                    autoFocus\n                                                />\n                                                <button onClick={handleDeckNameSave} className=\"text-green-600 hover:text-green-800 text-sm p-1\">‚úì Save</button>\n                                                <button onClick={handleDeckNameCancel} className=\"text-red-600 hover:text-red-800 text-sm p-1\">‚úó Cancel</button>\n                                            </div>\n                                        ) : (\n                                            // Display Mode\n                                            <div className=\"flex-grow flex items-center\">\n                                                <span className={`font-medium text-gray-800 mr-2 ${deck.id === selectedDeckId ? 'text-blue-600' : ''}`}>{deck.name}</span>\n                                                <span className=\"text-xs text-gray-500\">({deck.cards.length} cards)</span>\n                                                {deck.id === selectedDeckId && <span className=\"text-xs font-bold text-blue-600 ml-2\">(Selected)</span>}\n                                            </div>\n                                        )}\n\n                                        {/* Actions (only show if not editing this specific deck) */}\n                                        {editingDeckId !== deck.id && (\n                                            <div className=\"flex space-x-2 items-center flex-shrink-0 mt-2 sm:mt-0\">\n                                                <button\n                                                    onClick={() => handleSelectDeck(deck.id)}\n                                                    disabled={deck.id === selectedDeckId}\n                                                    className=\"px-2 py-1 bg-blue-500 text-white rounded hover:bg-blue-600 text-xs disabled:opacity-50 disabled:cursor-not-allowed\"\n                                                >\n                                                    Select\n                                                </button>\n                                                <button\n                                                    onClick={() => handleDeckNameEdit(deck.id)}\n                                                    className=\"px-2 py-1 bg-yellow-500 text-white rounded hover:bg-yellow-600 text-xs\"\n                                                >\n                                                    Rename\n                                                </button>\n                                                <button\n                                                    onClick={() => handleDeleteDeck(deck.id)}\n                                                    className=\"px-2 py-1 bg-red-500 text-white rounded hover:bg-red-600 text-xs\"\n                                                >\n                                                    Delete\n                                                </button>\n                                            </div>\n                                        )}\n                                    </li>\n                                ))}\n                            </ul>\n                        ) : (\n                            <p className=\"text-gray-500 text-center py-5\">No decks available. Upload one using the button above!</p>\n                        )}\n                    </div>\n                )}\n\n                {/* Settings View */}\n                {view === 'settings' && (\n                    <div>\n                        <h2 className=\"text-xl font-semibold mb-4 text-gray-700\">Settings</h2>\n                        <div className=\"space-y-6\">\n                            {/* Reset Scores for Current Deck */}\n                            <div className=\"p-4 border border-gray-200 rounded bg-gray-50\">\n                                <h3 className=\"font-medium mb-2 text-gray-600\">Reset Current Deck Progress</h3>\n                                {currentDeck ? (\n                                    <>\n                                        <p className=\"text-sm text-gray-500 mb-3\">This will reset correct/incorrect counts for all tags in the deck: \"{deckName}\".</p>\n                                        <button\n                                            onClick={resetCurrentDeckScores}\n                                            className=\"px-4 py-2 bg-yellow-500 text-white rounded hover:bg-yellow-600 text-sm\"\n                                        >\n                                            Reset Scores for \"{deckName}\"\n                                        </button>\n                                    </>\n                                ) : (\n                                    <p className=\"text-sm text-gray-500\">Select a deck first to reset its scores.</p>\n                                )}\n                            </div>\n\n                            {/* Clear All Data */}\n                            <div className=\"p-4 border border-red-300 rounded bg-red-50\">\n                                <h3 className=\"font-medium mb-2 text-red-700\">Danger Zone</h3>\n                                <p className=\"text-sm text-red-600 mb-3\">This will permanently delete ALL decks and ALL progress from your browser's storage.</p>\n                                <button\n                                    onClick={clearAllData}\n                                    className=\"px-4 py-2 bg-red-600 text-white rounded hover:bg-red-700 text-sm font-semibold\"\n                                >\n                                    Clear All Data\n                                </button>\n                            </div>\n                        </div>\n                    </div>\n                )}\n\n            </div>\n\n            {/* Footer/Info (Optional) */}\n            <footer className=\"text-center text-xs text-gray-400 mt-6\">\n                Flashcard App - Data stored in browser localStorage.\n            </footer>\n\n            {/* Global Styles for Flip Animation */}\n            <style jsx global>{`\n                .perspective { perspective: 1000px; }\n                .transform-style-3d { transform-style: preserve-3d; }\n                .backface-hidden { backface-visibility: hidden; -webkit-backface-visibility: hidden; }\n                .rotate-y-180 { transform: rotateY(180deg); }\n            `}</style>\n        </div>\n    );\n};\n\nexport default FlashcardApp;\n",
    "file_path": "/mnt/wsl/DebianProjectsVHD/workspace/projects/webapps/study-tools/src/components/NewApp.tsx"

üßë‚Äçüíª ## USER

wait, we were supposed to conduct planning first. we can't just vibe code this thing because that's falling out of fashion. let's create an architectural overview and a specification sheet with user stories and all that stuff to plan our sprint./

---

‚ú® ## MODEL

Understood, GG. My apologies for jumping the gun. A systematic approach is crucial for a project of this scope.

Here's a proposed plan for our architectural overview and specification sheet:

**Phase 1: Architectural Overview**

1.  **Current State:** Briefly describe the existing application's structure and technologies.
2.  **Proposed AI Integration:** Outline how AI agents will be incorporated, including potential new components (e.g., backend services) and their roles.
3.  **Data Flow:** Illustrate the interaction between the frontend, any new backend services, and AI models.

**Phase 2: Specification Sheet**

1.  **Core Problem/Goal:** Clearly define the overarching objective of this overhaul.
2.  **User Stories:** Detail specific functionalities from the user's perspective, focusing on AI-enhanced features.
3.  **Technical Requirements (High-Level):** List the key technical considerations and technologies needed for each user story.
4.  **Prioritization:** Assign priority levels to user stories and technical tasks.

---

**Initial Draft: Architectural Overview & Specification Sheet**

**1. Core Problem/Goal:**

To significantly enhance the flashcard application's intelligence and efficiency by integrating advanced AI agent capabilities, enabling more dynamic content generation, personalized learning paths, and intuitive user interactions.

**2. High-Level Architecture:**

*   **Frontend (Existing):** Next.js (React) application, responsible for UI and user interaction. Will be modified to communicate with a new backend for AI features.
*   **Backend (New):** A dedicated service (e.g., Node.js with Express.js or Python with FastAPI) to act as an intermediary between the frontend and AI models. This backend will:
    *   Expose RESTful API endpoints for AI-driven functionalities.
    *   Handle requests from the frontend, orchestrate calls to various AI models.
    *   Perform data pre-processing and post-processing for AI interactions.
    *   Manage API keys and credentials for external AI services (if used).
*   **AI Models:** A flexible layer to integrate with different AI models. Initially, this could involve external APIs (e.g., Google Gemini API). The architecture should allow for future transition to local models as per your long-term goal.
*   **Data Persistence (Existing & Enhanced):** Continue using `localStorage` for core flashcard data. The backend might introduce a database for more complex AI-related data or user preferences if needed for future features.

**3. Data Flow (Example for AI-driven Flashcard Generation):**

1.  User inputs text/topic into the frontend.
2.  Frontend sends a request to the Backend API (e.g., `POST /api/generate-flashcards`).
3.  Backend receives the request, prepares the prompt, and calls the AI Model API.
4.  AI Model processes the prompt and returns generated flashcard data (front, back, tags).
5.  Backend receives AI output, validates/formats it, and sends it back to the frontend.
6.  Frontend displays the newly generated flashcards to the user.

**4. User Stories (Initial Draft):**

**As a User, I want to...**

*   **US-1: AI-Powered Flashcard Generation from Text**
    *   ...paste a block of text (e.g., lecture notes, article) and have the AI automatically generate a set of flashcards (front, back, and relevant tags) from it, so I can quickly create study materials without manual effort.
*   **US-2: AI-Powered Flashcard Generation from Topic**
    *   ...provide a specific topic or concept (e.g., "Quantum Entanglement," "React Hooks") and have the AI generate a set of comprehensive flashcards related to that topic, so I can explore new subjects and build foundational knowledge efficiently.
*   **US-3: AI-Suggested Card Improvements**
    *   ...select an existing flashcard and ask the AI to suggest alternative phrasing for the front or back to improve clarity, conciseness, or accuracy, so my study materials are of higher quality.
*   **US-4: AI-Enhanced Tagging**
    *   ...have the AI analyze the content of my flashcards and suggest additional, relevant tags, so my cards are better organized and integrated into the spaced repetition system.
*   **US-5: AI-Driven Adaptive Learning Session**
    *   ...initiate a study session where the AI dynamically selects and orders cards based on my historical performance, learning patterns, and card difficulty, so I can optimize my learning and focus on areas needing improvement.
*   **US-6: AI-Powered Explanations/Summaries**
    *   ...click a button on the back of a flashcard to receive a more detailed explanation or a concise summary of the concept from the AI, so I can deepen my understanding beyond the basic answer.
*   **US-7: Natural Language Interface for Deck Management**
    *   ...be able to type natural language commands (e.g., "Show me all cards about JavaScript," "Create a new deck named 'My History Notes'") to manage my decks and cards, so I can interact with the application more intuitively.

**5. Technical Requirements (High-Level - to be detailed per story):**

*   Integration with AI APIs (e.g., Google Gemini, or local LLMs).
*   Frontend components for inputting text/topics and displaying AI output.
*   Backend API endpoints for each AI functionality.
*   Data validation and sanitization for AI inputs/outputs.
*   Error handling and user feedback mechanisms for AI interactions.
*   Potential database integration for storing AI-generated metadata or complex user learning profiles.

---

GG, please review this initial plan. Your feedback on the architectural direction and the proposed user stories is crucial. Which of these user stories are most important to you for the initial sprint? Are there any other AI-powered features you'd like to add or modify?

Project Overview\n\nThe Flashcard App is a web-based application designed to help users learn and memorize information through flashcards. It supports deck management, tag-based scoring, and an adaptive shuffling algorithm. The project is undergoing a significant overhaul to integrate advanced AI agent capabilities, aiming for dynamic content generation, personalized learning paths, and intuitive user interactions.\n\n## 2. Architectural Overview\n\nThe application follows a client-server architecture, with a Next.js frontend and a planned backend service for AI functionalities.\n\n### 2.1. Frontend (Next.js/React)\n\n*   **Technology:** Next.js (React), TypeScript, Tailwind CSS.\n*   **Responsibilities:**\n    *   User Interface (UI) and User Experience (UX).\n    *   Handling user interactions (e.g., card flipping, answering, deck management).\n    *   Displaying flashcards, stats, and settings.\n    *   Communicating with the AI Backend for AI-powered features.\n*   **Key Components:**\n    *   `src/app/page.tsx`: Main entry point for the application.\n    *   `src/components/NewApp.tsx`: The core Flashcard application component, which will be refactored into smaller, more manageable components and hooks.\n    *   `src/types/flashcard.d.ts`: TypeScript interface definitions for core data structures (Card, Deck, etc.).\n\n### 2.2. AI Backend (Planned)\n\n*   **Technology:** (To be decided, e.g., Node.js with Express.js or Python with FastAPI).\n*   **Responsibilities:**\n    *   Exposing RESTful API endpoints for AI functionalities (e.g., `/api/generate-flashcards`, `/api/suggest-tags`).\n    *   Orchestrating calls to various AI models (local or cloud-based).\n    *   Pre-processing user input for AI models and post-processing AI output.\n    *   Handling data validation and error handling for AI interactions.\n    *   Managing API keys and credentials for external AI services.\n*   **Data Flow (Example for AI-driven Flashcard Generation):**\n    1.  User inputs text/topic into the frontend.\n    2.  Frontend sends a request to the AI Backend API (e.g., `POST /api/generate-flashcards`).\n    3.  Backend receives the request, prepares the prompt, and calls the AI Model API.\n    4.  AI Model processes the prompt and returns generated flashcard data (front, back, tags).\n    5.  Backend receives AI output, validates/formats it, and sends it back to the frontend.\n    6.  Frontend displays the newly generated flashcards to the user.\n\n### 2.3. AI Models\n\n*   **Integration:** The architecture will support integration with various AI models. Initially, this may involve cloud-based LLM APIs (e.g., Google Gemini).\n*   **Future Goal:** Transition to local models for 95% of inference requests, as per project goals.\n\n## 3. Setup Instructions\n\n### 3.1. Prerequisites\n\n*   Node.js (LTS version recommended)\n*   npm or Yarn\n*   Git\n\n### 3.2. Getting Started\n\n1.  **Clone the repository:**\n    ```bash\n    git clone <repository-url>\n    cd study-tools\n    ```\n2.  **Install dependencies:**\n    ```bash\n    npm install\n    # or yarn install\n    ```\n3.  **Run the development server:**\n    ```bash\n    npm run dev\n    # or yarn dev\n    ```\n    Open [http://localhost:3000](http://localhost:3000) in your browser to see the application.\n\n## 4. AI Agent Integration Guidelines\n\nWhen developing new AI features, consider the following:\n\n*   **Modularity:** Keep AI-related logic separate from core UI components. Use custom hooks or dedicated utility functions.\n*   **Backend-First for AI:** All complex AI interactions (model calls, heavy processing) should go through the dedicated AI Backend service. The frontend should only consume the backend's API.\n*   **Error Handling:** Implement robust error handling for AI API calls, providing clear feedback to the user.\n*   **Scalability:** Design AI features with scalability in mind, considering potential future increases in usage or model complexity.\n*   **User Feedback:** Provide clear visual feedback to the user during AI processing (e.g., loading indicators).\n\n## 5. User Stories (Prioritized for Initial Sprint)\n\nHere are the user stories guiding our initial AI integration efforts:\n\n*   **US-1: AI-Powered Flashcard Generation from Text**\n    *   **Description:** As a user, I want to paste a block of text (e.g., lecture notes, article) and have the AI automatically generate a set of flashcards (front, back, and relevant tags) from it, so I can quickly create study materials without manual effort.\n*   **US-2: AI-Powered Flashcard Generation from Topic**\n    *   **Description:** As a user, I want to provide a specific topic or concept (e.g., \"Quantum Entanglement,\" \"React Hooks\") and have the AI generate a set of comprehensive flashcards related to that topic, so I can explore new subjects and build foundational knowledge efficiently.\n*   **US-3: AI-Suggested Card Improvements**\n    *   **Description:** As a user, I want to select an existing flashcard and ask the AI to suggest alternative phrasing for the front or back to improve clarity, conciseness, or accuracy, so my study materials are of higher quality.\n\nFurther user stories will be prioritized in subsequent sprints.\n"
  }
}

    "output": "# Simple Next.js Flashcard App\n\nA minimal flashcard application built with Next.js, React, and Tailwind CSS. It allows you to:\n\n*   Study flashcards using a simple interface.\n*   Mark cards as correct or incorrect.\n*   Shuffle decks based on tag performance (shows weaker tags more often).\n*   View basic statistics on tag performance.\n*   Upload your own decks in JSON format.\n*   Manage multiple decks (select, rename, delete).\n\n**Important:** This app stores all data (decks, cards, scores) directly in your web browser's `localStorage`. There is no backend server or database.\n\n## Prerequisites\n\nBefore you begin, ensure you have the following installed on your system:\n\n*   **Node.js:** (LTS version recommended). You can download it from [nodejs.org](https://nodejs.org/). Verify installation by running `node -v` in your terminal.\n*   **npm** (comes with Node.js) or **yarn:** Verify installation with `npm -v` or `yarn -v`.\n*   **Git:** Needed to clone the repository. Verify installation with `git --version`.\n\n## Getting Started\n\nFollow these steps to get the project running on your local machine:\n\n1.  **Clone the Repository:**\n    Open your terminal or command prompt and run:\n    ```bash\n    git clone https://github.com/C-Vac/nextjs-flashcards\n    ```\n\n2.  **Navigate to Project Directory:**\n    Change into the newly cloned folder:\n    ```bash\n    cd nextjs-flashcards\n    ```\n\n3.  **Install Dependencies:**\n    Install the necessary Node.js packages using npm or yarn:\n    ```bash\n    npm install\n    # OR\n    yarn install\n    ```\n\n4.  **Run the Development Server:**\n    Start the Next.js development server:\n    ```bash\n    npm run dev\n    # OR\n    yarn dev\n    ```\n\n5.  **Open the App:**\n    Open your web browser and navigate to [http://localhost:3000](http://localhost:3000). You should see the flashcard application.\n\n## How to Use\n\n1.  **Initial View:** The app might start with a default sample deck.\n2.  **Studying:**\n    *   The \"Viewer\" tab shows the current card.\n    *   Click the card or the \"Flip Card\" button to see the back.\n    *   Click \"Correct\" or \"Incorrect\" to record your answer and move to the next card.\n    *   The deck is shuffled to show cards with tags you get wrong more often first. Click \"Shuffle Deck\" to reshuffle anytime.\n3.  **Uploading Your Deck (e.g., ML Concepts):**\n    *   Go to the \"Manage Decks\" tab.\n    *   Click \"Choose JSON File...\".\n    *   Select the JSON file containing your flashcards (from the `decks` folder).\n    *   The deck will be uploaded, added to the list, and automatically selected for studying.\n4.  **Managing Decks:**\n    *   In \"Manage Decks\", you can see all uploaded decks.\n    *   Click \"Select\" to choose a different deck to study.\n    *   Click \"Rename\" to change a deck's name.\n    *   Click \"Delete\" to remove a deck (and its scores) permanently *from this browser*.\n5.  **Viewing Stats:**\n    *   The \"Stats\" tab shows your performance (correct/incorrect percentage) for each tag within the *currently selected* deck. Weakest tags are listed first.\n    *   You can reset the score for individual tags here.\n6.  **Settings:**\n    *   The \"Settings\" tab allows you to reset all scores for the currently selected deck or clear *all* data (all decks, all scores) stored by the app in your browser. **Use with caution!**\n\n## Data Storage Notice\n\n*   All your decks and study progress are saved *only* in your browser's `localStorage`.\n*   This means the data is tied to the specific browser you are using on your specific computer.\n*   If you clear your browser's data/cache/storage, **you will lose all your flashcards and progress.**\n*   Data will not sync across different browsers or different computers.\n*   Using Incognito or Private Browsing mode will likely mean data is lost when you close the window.\n\n---\n\nHappy studying!\n"
  }
}
```

You should see the flashcard application.\n\n## How to Use\n\n1.  **Initial View:** The app might start with a default sample deck.\n2.  **Studying:**\n    *   The \"Viewer\" tab shows the current card.\n    *   Click the card or the \"Flip Card\" button to see the back.\n    *   Click \"Correct\" or \"Incorrect\" to record your answer and move to the next card.\n    *   The deck is shuffled to show cards with tags you get wrong more often first. Click \"Shuffle Deck\" to reshuffle anytime.\n3.  **Uploading Your Deck (e.g., ML Concepts):**\n    *   Go to the \"Manage Decks\" tab.\n    *   Click \"Choose JSON File...\".\n    *   Select the JSON file containing your flashcards (from the `decks` folder).\n    *   The deck will be uploaded, added to the list, and automatically selected for studying.\n4.  **Managing Decks:**\n    *   In \"Manage Decks\", you can see all uploaded decks.\n    *   Click \"Select\" to choose a different deck to study.\n    *   Click \"Rename\" to change a deck's name.\n    *   Click \"Delete\" to remove a deck (and its scores) permanently *from this browser*.\n5.  **Viewing Stats:**\n    *   The \"Stats\" tab shows your performance (correct/incorrect percentage) for each tag within the *currently selected* deck. Weakest tags are listed first.\n    *   You can reset the score for individual tags here.\n6.  **Settings:**\n    *   The \"Settings\" tab allows you to reset all scores for the currently selected deck or clear *all* data (all decks, all scores) stored by the app in your browser. **Use with caution!**\n\n## Data Storage Notice\n\n*   All your decks and study progress are saved *only* in your browser's `localStorage`.\n*   This means the data is tied to the specific browser you are using on your specific computer.\n*   If you clear your browser's data/cache/storage, **you will lose all your flashcards and progress.**\n*   Data will not sync across different browsers or different computers.\n*   Using Incognito or Private Browsing mode will likely mean data is lost when you close the window.\n\n---\n\nHappy studying!\n",
    "new_string": "# Simple Next.js Flashcard App\n\nA minimal flashcard application built with Next.js, React, and Tailwind CSS. It allows you to:\n\n*   Study flashcards using a simple interface.\n*   Mark cards as correct or incorrect.\n*   Shuffle decks based on tag performance (shows weaker tags more often).\n*   View basic statistics on tag performance.\n*   Upload your own decks in JSON format.\n*   Manage multiple decks (select, rename, delete).\n\n**Important:** This app stores all data (decks, cards, scores) directly in your web browser's `localStorage`. There is no backend server or database.\n\n## Prerequisites\n\nBefore you begin, ensure you have the following installed on your system:\n\n*   **Node.js:** (LTS version recommended). You can download it from [nodejs.org](https://nodejs.org/). Verify installation by running `node -v` in your terminal.\n*   **npm** (comes with Node.js) or **yarn:** Verify installation with `npm -v` or `yarn -v`.\n*   **Git:** Needed to clone the repository. Verify installation with `git --version`.\n\n## Getting Started\n\nFollow these steps to get the project running on your local machine:\n\n1.  **Clone the Repository:**\n    Open your terminal or command prompt and run:\n    ```bash\n    git clone https://github.com/C-Vac/nextjs-flashcards\n    ```\n\n2.  **Navigate to Project Directory:**\n    Change into the newly cloned folder:\n    ```bash\n    cd nextjs-flashcards\n    ```\n\n3.  **Install Dependencies:**\n    Install the necessary Node.js packages using npm or yarn:\n    ```bash\n    npm install\n    # OR\n    yarn install\n    ```\n\n4.  **Run the Development Server:**\n    Start the Next.js development server:\n    ```bash\n    npm run dev\n    # OR\n    yarn dev\n    ```\n\n5.  **Open the App:**\n    Open your web browser and navigate to [http://localhost:3000](http://localhost:3000). You should see the flashcard application.\n\n## How to Use\n\n1.  **Initial View:** The app might start with a default sample deck.\n2.  **Studying:**\n    *   The \"Viewer\" tab shows the current card.\n    *   Click the card or the \"Flip Card\" button to see the back.\n    *   Click \"Correct\" or \"Incorrect\" to record your answer and move to the next card.\n    *   The deck is shuffled to show cards with tags you get wrong more often first. Click \"Shuffle Deck\" to reshuffle anytime.\n3.  **Uploading Your Deck (e.g., ML Concepts):**\n    *   Go to the \"Manage Decks\" tab.\n    *   Click \"Choose JSON File...\".\n    *   Select the JSON file containing your flashcards (from the `decks` folder).\n    *   The deck will be uploaded, added to the list, and automatically selected for studying.\n4.  **Managing Decks:**\n    *   In \"Manage Decks\", you can see all uploaded decks.\n    *   Click \"Select\" to choose a different deck to study.\n    *   Click \"Rename\" to change a deck's name.\n    *   Click \"Delete\" to remove a deck (and its scores) permanently *from this browser*.\n5.  **Viewing Stats:**\n    *   The \"Stats\" tab shows your performance (correct/incorrect percentage) for each tag within the *currently selected* deck. Weakest tags are listed first.\n    *   You can reset the score for individual tags here.\n6.  **Settings:**\n    *   The \"Settings\" tab allows you to reset all scores for the currently selected deck or clear *all* data (all decks, all scores) stored by the app in your browser. **Use with caution!**\n\n## Data Storage Notice\n\n*   All your decks and study progress are saved *only* in your browser's `localStorage`.\n*   This means the data is tied to the specific browser you are using on your specific computer.\n*   If you clear your browser's data/cache/storage, **you will lose all your flashcards and progress.**\n*   Data will not sync across different browsers or different computers.\n    *   Using Incognito or Private Browsing mode will likely mean data is lost when you close the window.\n\n## AI-Powered Features (Under Development)\n\nThis application is actively being enhanced with advanced AI capabilities to provide a more intelligent and personalized learning experience. Future updates will include features such as AI-driven flashcard generation from text or topics, AI-suggested card improvements, and adaptive learning sessions.\n\nFor developers interested in contributing to these new features or understanding the AI integration, please refer to the [`DEVELOPMENT.md`](./DEVELOPMENT.md) guide.\n\n---\n\nHappy studying!\n\n",

(will be loaded if no data exists) ---\nconst createDefaultDeck = (): Deck => ({\n    id: 'default_deck_1',\n    name: 'Sample React/Web Dev Deck',\n    cards: [\n        { id: 1, front: \"What is
